æ‰¿çŸ¥ã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼ç¾åœ¨ã®tours-content.jsonã‚’æ›´ã«åˆ†å‰²ã™ã‚‹ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ã€‚

```javascript
import fs from 'fs';

// ç¾åœ¨ã®tours-content.jsonã‚’èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
const toursContent = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-content.json', 'utf8'));

// æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’åé›†ã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã‚’ä½œæˆ
const mediaItems = new Map(); // é‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ç”¨
let mediaIdCounter = 1;

// 1. tours-extra-notes.jsonï¼ˆextraNotesã®ã¿ï¼‰
const toursExtraNotes = toursContent.map(tour => ({
  id: tour.id,
  extraNotes: tour.extraNotes || ""
}));

// 2. æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’è§£æã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’æ§‹ç¯‰
toursContent.forEach(tour => {
  // liveVideosã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const key = video.title + '|' + video.type;
        if (!mediaItems.has(key)) {
          mediaItems.set(key, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: video.title,
            type: video.type,
            category: 'liveVideo',
            links: video.links || []
          });
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const key = videoTitle.trim() + '|unknown';
        if (!mediaItems.has(key)) {
          mediaItems.set(key, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: videoTitle.trim(),
            type: 'unknown',
            category: 'liveVideo',
            links: []
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const key = arrangement.notes + '|arrangement';
        if (!mediaItems.has(key)) {
          mediaItems.set(key, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: arrangement.notes,
            type: 'note',
            category: 'liveArrangement',
            links: []
          });
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const key = arrangementTitle.trim() + '|arrangement';
        if (!mediaItems.has(key)) {
          mediaItems.set(key, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: arrangementTitle.trim(),
            type: 'note',
            category: 'liveArrangement',
            links: []
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }
});

// 3. media-master.jsonï¼ˆæ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ï¼‰
const mediaMaster = Array.from(mediaItems.values());

// 4. tours-media.jsonï¼ˆå‚ç…§é–¢ä¿‚ï¼‰
const toursMedia = toursContent.map(tour => {
  const result = {
    id: tour.id,
    liveVideoIds: [],
    liveArrangementIds: []
  };

  // liveVideosã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const key = video.title + '|' + video.type;
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(key);
        if (mediaItem) {
          result.liveVideoIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const key = videoTitle.trim() + '|unknown';
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(key);
        if (mediaItem) {
          result.liveVideoIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const key = arrangement.notes + '|arrangement';
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(key);
        if (mediaItem) {
          result.liveArrangementIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const key = arrangementTitle.trim() + '|arrangement';
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(key);
        if (mediaItem) {
          result.liveArrangementIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  return result;
});

// ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«å‡ºåŠ›
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/media-master.json', JSON.stringify(mediaMaster, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-media.json', JSON.stringify(toursMedia, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-extra-notes.json', JSON.stringify(toursExtraNotes, null, 2));

console.log('tours-content.jsonã®åˆ†å‰²ãŒå®Œäº†ã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼š');
console.log('- public/data/media-master.json');
console.log('- public/data/tours-media.json');
console.log('- public/data/tours-extra-notes.json');
console.log(`æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã«${mediaMaster.length}ä»¶ã®ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚`);
```

ãƒ»ä»Šå›ã®å¯¾å¿œã«ã‚ˆã‚Šã€"liveVideo"ã€€ã¨ã€€"liveArrangement"ã€€ã®ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãƒ¼åˆ†ã‘ã¯ä¸è¦ã«ãªã‚‹ã¯ãšã§ã™ã€‚

## **ä¿®æ­£ç‚¹ã«ã¤ã„ã¦**

### **1. categoryãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã®å‰Šé™¤**
ç¢ºã‹ã«åŒã˜æ˜ åƒã‚’ä¸¡æ–¹ã®ç”¨é€”ã§ä½¿ç”¨ã™ã‚‹ãªã‚‰ã€ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªãƒ¼åˆ†ã‘ã¯ä¸è¦ã§ã™ã­ã€‚

### **2. é‡è¤‡é …ç›®ã®å•é¡Œ**
ç¾åœ¨ã®media-master.jsonã§é‡è¤‡ã‚’ç¢ºèªã™ã‚‹ã¨ï¼š
- "T.M.Revolution DVD Series The Summary -summarize 1-" (media1, media4)
- "ç„¡ã—" (media3, media7) 
- "T.M.Revolution SEVENTH HEAVEN T.M.R. LIVE REVOLUTION'04" (media17, media18)

### **3. "id"é …ç›®åã«ã¤ã„ã¦**
**å•é¡Œã‚ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“**ã€‚ç†ç”±ï¼š
- `tours-core.json`ã®`id`ã¯**ãƒ„ã‚¢ãƒ¼ID**ï¼ˆæ•°å€¤ï¼‰
- `media-master.json`ã®`id`ã¯**ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ID**ï¼ˆæ–‡å­—åˆ—ï¼‰
- ç•°ãªã‚‹ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ç¨®åˆ¥ãªã®ã§åå‰ç©ºé–“ãŒåˆ†é›¢ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹

### **4. ä¿®æ­£ç‰ˆã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆ**

é‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ã¨categoryå‰Šé™¤ã‚’è¡Œã†ä¿®æ­£ç‰ˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript
import fs from 'fs';

// ç¾åœ¨ã®tours-content.jsonã‚’èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
const toursContent = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-content.json', 'utf8'));

// æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’åé›†ã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã‚’ä½œæˆï¼ˆé‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ï¼‰
const mediaItems = new Map(); // titleãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã§é‡è¤‡æ’é™¤
let mediaIdCounter = 1;

// 1. tours-extra-notes.jsonï¼ˆextraNotesã®ã¿ï¼‰
const toursExtraNotes = toursContent.map(tour => ({
  id: tour.id,
  extraNotes: tour.extraNotes || ""
}));

// 2. æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’è§£æã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’æ§‹ç¯‰ï¼ˆé‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ï¼‰
toursContent.forEach(tour => {
  // liveVideosã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const title = video.title.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: video.type || 'unknown',
            links: video.links || []
          });
        } else {
          // æ—¢å­˜ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã®linksã‚’æ›´æ–°ï¼ˆã‚ˆã‚Šè©³ç´°ãªæƒ…å ±ãŒã‚ã‚Œã°ï¼‰
          const existing = mediaItems.get(title);
          if (video.links && video.links.length > 0 && existing.links.length === 0) {
            existing.links = video.links;
            existing.type = video.type || existing.type;
          }
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const title = videoTitle.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: 'unknown',
            links: []
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const title = arrangement.notes.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: 'note',
            links: []
          });
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const title = arrangementTitle.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: 'note',
            links: []
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }
});

// 3. media-master.jsonï¼ˆæ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã€categoryãªã—ã€é‡è¤‡ãªã—ï¼‰
const mediaMaster = Array.from(mediaItems.values());

// 4. tours-media.jsonï¼ˆå‚ç…§é–¢ä¿‚ã€æ–°ã—ã„IDã§æ›´æ–°ï¼‰
const toursMedia = toursContent.map(tour => {
  const result = {
    id: tour.id,
    mediaIds: [] // liveVideoIdsã¨liveArrangementIdsã‚’çµ±åˆ
  };

  // liveVideosã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const title = video.title.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.mediaIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.mediaIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const title = videoTitle.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.mediaIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.mediaIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const title = arrangement.notes.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.mediaIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.mediaIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const title = arrangementTitle.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.mediaIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.mediaIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  return result;
});

// ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«å‡ºåŠ›
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/media-master.json', JSON.stringify(mediaMaster, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-media.json', JSON.stringify(toursMedia, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-extra-notes.json', JSON.stringify(toursExtraNotes, null, 2));

console.log('ä¿®æ­£ç‰ˆã®åˆ†å‰²ãŒå®Œäº†ã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼š');
console.log('- public/data/media-master.json');
console.log('- public/data/tours-media.json');  
console.log('- public/data/tours-extra-notes.json');

## **Step 1: æ–°ã—ã„å‹å®šç¾©ã®ä½œæˆ**

  id: string;
  title: string;
  type: string;
  links: string[];
};

  id: number;
  mediaIds: string[];

## **Step 2: ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚µãƒ¼ãƒ“ã‚¹ã®ä½œæˆ**

```typescript
import { Tour } from '../types/tour';
import { MediaItem, TourMedia, TourExtraNotes, TourCore, Setlist } from '../types/media';

export async function loadToursData(): Promise<Tour[]> {
  const version = import.meta.env?.VITE_APP_VERSION || Date.now();
  
  try {
    // ä¸¦è¡Œã—ã¦ã™ã¹ã¦ã®JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‚’å–å¾—
    const [
      toursCore,
      setlists,
      mediaMaster,
      toursMedia,
      toursExtraNotes
    ] = await Promise.all([
      fetch(`data/tours-core.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourCore[]>,
      fetch(`data/setlists.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<Setlist[]>,
      fetch(`data/media-master.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<MediaItem[]>,
      fetch(`data/tours-media.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourMedia[]>,
      fetch(`data/tours-extra-notes.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourExtraNotes[]>
    ]);

    // ã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ‡ãƒƒã‚¯ã‚¹ãƒãƒƒãƒ—ã‚’ä½œæˆï¼ˆé«˜é€ŸåŒ–ã®ãŸã‚ï¼‰
    const setlistMap = new Map(setlists.map(s => [s.tourId, s.songs]));
    const mediaMap = new Map(mediaMaster.map(m => [m.id, m]));
    const tourMediaMap = new Map(toursMedia.map(tm => [tm.id, tm.mediaIds]));
    const extraNotesMap = new Map(toursExtraNotes.map(en => [en.id, en.extraNotes]));

    // ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’çµåˆã—ã¦Touré…åˆ—ã‚’ä½œæˆ
    const tours: Tour[] = toursCore.map(core => {
      const setlist = setlistMap.get(core.id);
      const mediaIds = tourMediaMap.get(core.id) || [];
      const extraNotes = extraNotesMap.get(core.id) || '';

      // ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢æƒ…å ±ã‚’å–å¾—
      const mediaItems = mediaIds.map(id => mediaMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean) as MediaItem[];
      
      // liveVideosã¨liveArrangementsã«åˆ†ã‘ã‚‹å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚‹å ´åˆã®å‡¦ç†
      // ç¾åœ¨ã¯çµ±åˆã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹ã®ã§ã€å¿…è¦ã«å¿œã˜ã¦åˆ†ã‘ã‚‹
      const liveVideos = mediaItems.filter(m => 
        m.type !== 'note' && !m.title.includes('(CD)')
      );
      const liveArrangements = mediaItems.filter(m => 
        m.type === 'note' || m.title.includes('(CD)')
      );

      return {
        id: core.id,
        title: core.title,
        subtitle: core.subtitle,
        year: core.year,
        description: core.description,
        setlist: setlist || [],
        extraNotes,
        // å¾“æ¥ã®å½¢å¼ã«åˆã‚ã›ã¦liveVideosã‚’æ–‡å­—åˆ—é…åˆ—ã¨ã—ã¦æ§‹ç¯‰
        liveVideos: liveVideos.length > 0 ? liveVideos.map(v => v.title).join('\n') : undefined,
        liveArrangements: liveArrangements.length > 0 ? liveArrangements.map(a => a.title).join('\n') : undefined,
        // å¿…è¦ã«å¿œã˜ã¦ä»–ã®ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã‚‚è¿½åŠ 
        memo: '',
        releases: []
      };
    });

    return tours;

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to load tours data:', error);
    // ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒãƒƒã‚¯: å¾“æ¥ã®tours.jsonã‚’è©¦ã™
    try {
      const fallbackData = await fetch(`tours.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json());
      console.warn('Using fallback tours.json');
      return fallbackData;
    } catch (fallbackError) {
      console.error('Fallback also failed:', fallbackError);
      return [];
    }
  }
}

// ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢æƒ…å ±ã‚’å–å¾—ã™ã‚‹ãƒ˜ãƒ«ãƒ‘ãƒ¼é–¢æ•°
export async function getMediaItems(mediaIds: string[]): Promise<MediaItem[]> {
  const version = import.meta.env?.VITE_APP_VERSION || Date.now();
  
  try {
    const mediaMaster = await fetch(`data/media-master.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as MediaItem[];
    const mediaMap = new Map(mediaMaster.map(m => [m.id, m]));
    
    return mediaIds.map(id => mediaMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean) as MediaItem[];
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to load media data:', error);
    return [];
  }
}
```

      .then((data: Tour[]) => {
        setTours(data);
        setFiltered(data);

        setFiltered([]);

## **Step 4: ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãŒæ­£ã—ãèª­ã¿è¾¼ã¾ã‚Œã‚‹ã‹ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆ**

PowerShellã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒå‡ºã¾ã—ãŸãŒã€åˆ¥ã®æ–¹æ³•ã§ç¢ºèªã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

ãƒ“ãƒ«ãƒ‰ãŒæˆåŠŸã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼æ¬¡ã«ã€å®Ÿéš›ã«ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãŒæ­£ã—ãèª­ã¿è¾¼ã¾ã‚Œã‚‹ã‹ã‚’ç¢ºèªã™ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã€ç°¡å˜ãªãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript
// Node.jsç’°å¢ƒã§ã®ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆç”¨ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆ
import fs from 'fs';

// ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ãŒå­˜åœ¨ã™ã‚‹ã‹ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
const requiredFiles = [
  'public/data/tours-core.json',
  'public/data/setlists.json',
  'public/data/media-master.json',
  'public/data/tours-media.json',
  'public/data/tours-extra-notes.json'
];

console.log('ğŸ” Checking required data files...');
for (const file of requiredFiles) {
  if (fs.existsSync(file)) {
    const stats = fs.statSync(file);
    console.log(`âœ… ${file} (${(stats.size / 1024).toFixed(1)}KB)`);
  } else {
    console.log(`âŒ ${file} - Missing!`);
  }
}

// ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®åŸºæœ¬æ§‹é€ ã‚’ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
console.log('\nğŸ“Š Data structure validation...');

try {
  const toursCore = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-core.json', 'utf8'));
  const setlists = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/setlists.json', 'utf8'));
  const mediaMaster = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/media-master.json', 'utf8'));
  const toursMedia = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-media.json', 'utf8'));
  const toursExtraNotes = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-extra-notes.json', 'utf8'));

  console.log(`âœ… tours-core: ${toursCore.length} items`);
  console.log(`âœ… setlists: ${setlists.length} items`);
  console.log(`âœ… media-master: ${mediaMaster.length} items`);
  console.log(`âœ… tours-media: ${toursMedia.length} items`);
  console.log(`âœ… tours-extra-notes: ${toursExtraNotes.length} items`);

  // IDç¯„å›²ã‚’ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
  const coreIds = toursCore.map(t => t.id).sort((a, b) => a - b);
  const setlistIds = setlists.map(s => s.tourId).sort((a, b) => a - b);
  
  console.log(`\nğŸ” ID ranges:`);
  console.log(`   Tours: ${coreIds[0]} - ${coreIds[coreIds.length - 1]}`);
  console.log(`   Setlists: ${setlistIds[0]} - ${setlistIds[setlistIds.length - 1]}`);

  // æœ€åˆã®ãƒ„ã‚¢ãƒ¼ã®çµåˆä¾‹
  console.log(`\nğŸ”— Sample merged data for Tour #1:`);
  const tour1Core = toursCore.find(t => t.id === 1);
  const tour1Setlist = setlists.find(s => s.tourId === 1);
  const tour1Media = toursMedia.find(tm => tm.id === 1);
  const tour1Notes = toursExtraNotes.find(en => en.id === 1);

  if (tour1Core) {
    console.log(`   Title: ${tour1Core.title} ${tour1Core.subtitle}`);
    console.log(`   Description: ${tour1Core.description.substring(0, 50)}...`);
    if (tour1Setlist) {
      console.log(`   Songs: ${tour1Setlist.songs.length} tracks`);
    }
    if (tour1Media && tour1Media.mediaIds.length > 0) {
      const mediaItems = tour1Media.mediaIds.map(id => 
        mediaMaster.find(m => m.id === id)
      ).filter(Boolean);
      console.log(`   Media: ${mediaItems.length} items`);
      mediaItems.slice(0, 2).forEach(item => {
        console.log(`     - ${item.title} (${item.type})`);
      });
    }
    if (tour1Notes && tour1Notes.extraNotes) {
      console.log(`   Notes: ${tour1Notes.extraNotes.substring(0, 50)}...`);
    }
  }

  console.log('\nâœ… All data files are valid and properly structured!');

} catch (error) {
  console.error('âŒ Error validating data structure:', error.message);
}
```

ç´ æ™´ã‚‰ã—ã„ï¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã¯æ­£å¸¸ã«èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¾ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚æ¬¡ã«ã€å®Ÿéš›ã«Webã‚¢ãƒ—ãƒªã‚±ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ã§å‹•ä½œã™ã‚‹ã‹ãƒ–ãƒ©ã‚¦ã‚¶ã§ç¢ºèªã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚ã¾ãšã€é–‹ç™ºã‚µãƒ¼ãƒãƒ¼ã‚’èµ·å‹•ã—ã¦ç¢ºèªã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

å‹•ä½œç¢ºèªã®ãŸã‚ã«ã€è©³ç´°ãªãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’è¿½åŠ ã—ã¦ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

```typescript
import type { Tour } from '../types/tour';
import type { MediaItem, TourMedia, TourExtraNotes, TourCore, Setlist } from '../types/media';

export async function loadToursData(): Promise<Tour[]> {
  const version = import.meta.env?.VITE_APP_VERSION || Date.now();
  
  console.log('ğŸ”„ Loading tours data from split files...');
  
  try {
    // ä¸¦è¡Œã—ã¦ã™ã¹ã¦ã®JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‚’å–å¾—
    console.log('ğŸ“¥ Fetching data files...');
    const [
      toursCore,
      setlists,
      mediaMaster,
      toursMedia,
      toursExtraNotes
    ] = await Promise.all([
      fetch(`data/tours-core.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourCore[]>,
      fetch(`data/setlists.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<Setlist[]>,
      fetch(`data/media-master.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<MediaItem[]>,
      fetch(`data/tours-media.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourMedia[]>,
      fetch(`data/tours-extra-notes.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourExtraNotes[]>
    ]);

    console.log(`âœ… Data loaded: ${toursCore.length} tours, ${setlists.length} setlists, ${mediaMaster.length} media items`);

    // ã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ‡ãƒƒã‚¯ã‚¹ãƒãƒƒãƒ—ã‚’ä½œæˆï¼ˆé«˜é€ŸåŒ–ã®ãŸã‚ï¼‰
    const setlistMap = new Map(setlists.map(s => [s.tourId, s.songs]));
    const mediaMap = new Map(mediaMaster.map(m => [m.id, m]));
    const tourMediaMap = new Map(toursMedia.map(tm => [tm.id, tm.mediaIds]));
    const extraNotesMap = new Map(toursExtraNotes.map(en => [en.id, en.extraNotes]));

    // ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’çµåˆã—ã¦Touré…åˆ—ã‚’ä½œæˆ
    console.log('ğŸ”— Merging data...');
    const tours: Tour[] = toursCore.map(core => {
      const setlist = setlistMap.get(core.id);
      const mediaIds = tourMediaMap.get(core.id) || [];
      const extraNotes = extraNotesMap.get(core.id) || '';

      // ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢æƒ…å ±ã‚’å–å¾—
      const mediaItems = mediaIds.map(id => mediaMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean) as MediaItem[];
      
      // liveVideosã¨liveArrangementsã«åˆ†ã‘ã‚‹å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚‹å ´åˆã®å‡¦ç†
      // ç¾åœ¨ã¯çµ±åˆã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹ã®ã§ã€å¿…è¦ã«å¿œã˜ã¦åˆ†ã‘ã‚‹
      const liveVideos = mediaItems.filter(m => 
        m.type !== 'note' && !m.title.includes('(CD)')
      );
      const liveArrangements = mediaItems.filter(m => 
        m.type === 'note' || m.title.includes('(CD)')
      );

      return {
        id: core.id,
        title: core.title,
        subtitle: core.subtitle,
        year: core.year,
        description: core.description,
        setlist: setlist || [],
        extraNotes,
        // å¾“æ¥ã®å½¢å¼ã«åˆã‚ã›ã¦liveVideosã‚’æ–‡å­—åˆ—é…åˆ—ã¨ã—ã¦æ§‹ç¯‰
        liveVideos: liveVideos.length > 0 ? liveVideos.map(v => v.title).join('\n') : undefined,
        liveArrangements: liveArrangements.length > 0 ? liveArrangements.map(a => a.title).join('\n') : undefined,
        // å¿…è¦ã«å¿œã˜ã¦ä»–ã®ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã‚‚è¿½åŠ 
        memo: '',
        releases: []
      };
    });

    console.log(`âœ… Successfully merged ${tours.length} tours`);
    return tours;

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ Failed to load tours data:', error);
    // ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒãƒƒã‚¯: å¾“æ¥ã®tours.jsonã‚’è©¦ã™
    try {
      console.log('ğŸ”„ Trying fallback tours.json...');
      const fallbackData = await fetch(`tours.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json());
      console.warn('âš ï¸ Using fallback tours.json');
      return fallbackData;
    } catch (fallbackError) {
      console.error('âŒ Fallback also failed:', fallbackError);
      return [];
    }
  }
}

// ... existing code ...
```

## **Step 5: ãƒ“ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã—ã¦å‹•ä½œç¢ºèª**

## **Step 6: ä¸è¦ã«ãªã£ãŸãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ³ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—**

## **âœ… å®Ÿè£…å®Œäº†ãƒ¬ãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆ**

### **ğŸ¯ å®Ÿè£…ã—ãŸå†…å®¹**

1. **æ–°ã—ã„å‹å®šç¾©ã®ä½œæˆ**

2. **ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚µãƒ¼ãƒ“ã‚¹ã®å®Ÿè£…**
   - `src/services/dataService.ts`: åˆ†å‰²ã•ã‚ŒãŸJSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‚’çµåˆã™ã‚‹ã‚µãƒ¼ãƒ“ã‚¹

   - ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒãƒƒã‚¯æ©Ÿèƒ½ï¼ˆå¾“æ¥ã®tours.jsonã¸ã®è‡ªå‹•åˆ‡ã‚Šæ›¿ãˆï¼‰
   - è©³ç´°ãªãƒ­ã‚°å‡ºåŠ›ã§ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°æ”¯æ´

3. **ãƒ¡ã‚¤ãƒ³ã‚¢ãƒ—ãƒªã‚±ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ã®æ›´æ–°**
   - `src/App.tsx`: æ–°ã—ã„ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚µãƒ¼ãƒ“ã‚¹ã‚’ä½¿ç”¨
   - å‹ã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆã®ä¿®æ­£

4. **ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿æ•´åˆæ€§ã®ç¢ºèª**

  m.type !== 'note' && !m.title.includes('(CD)')
);

  m.type === 'note' || m.title.includes('(CD)')

```

å•é¡Œã‚’ç‰¹å®šã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼ç¾åœ¨ã®ãƒ­ã‚¸ãƒƒã‚¯ã§ã¯ã€ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’`type`ã ã‘ã§åˆ†é¡ã—ã¦ã„ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã€å…ƒã€…ã®`liveVideos`ã¨`liveArrangements`ã®åŒºåˆ¥ãŒå¤±ã‚ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚

å…ƒã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿æ§‹é€ ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ä¿®æ­£ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚

å•é¡ŒãŒåˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸï¼å…ƒãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®`liveVideos`ã¨`liveArrangements`ã®åˆ†é¡ã‚’ä¿æŒã™ã‚‹å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ã€‚

ç¾åœ¨ã®`split-content-fixed.js`ã¯å…ƒã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’**åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’å¤±ã£ã¦**çµåˆã—ã¦ã—ã¾ã£ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚

## **ğŸ”§ ä¿®æ­£æ–¹æ³•**

`split-content-fixed.js`ã‚’ä¿®æ­£ã—ã¦ã€ã©ã®ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ãŒå…ƒã€…`liveVideos`ã«å±ã—ã¦ã„ãŸã‹ã€`liveArrangements`ã«å±ã—ã¦ã„ãŸã‹ã®æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒã™ã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã«ã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript
import fs from 'fs';

// ç¾åœ¨ã®tours-content.jsonã‚’èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
const toursContent = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-content.json', 'utf8'));

// æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’åé›†ã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã‚’ä½œæˆï¼ˆé‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ï¼‰
const mediaItems = new Map(); // titleãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã§é‡è¤‡æ’é™¤
let mediaIdCounter = 1;

// 1. tours-extra-notes.jsonï¼ˆextraNotesã®ã¿ï¼‰
const toursExtraNotes = toursContent.map(tour => ({
  id: tour.id,
  extraNotes: tour.extraNotes || ""
}));

// 2. æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’è§£æã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’æ§‹ç¯‰ï¼ˆé‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ã€åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ä¿æŒï¼‰
toursContent.forEach(tour => {
  // liveVideosã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const title = video.title.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: video.type || 'unknown',
            links: video.links || [],
            category: 'liveVideo' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        } else {
          // æ—¢å­˜ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã®linksã‚’æ›´æ–°ï¼ˆã‚ˆã‚Šè©³ç´°ãªæƒ…å ±ãŒã‚ã‚Œã°ï¼‰
          const existing = mediaItems.get(title);
          if (video.links && video.links.length > 0 && existing.links.length === 0) {
            existing.links = video.links;
            existing.type = video.type || existing.type;
          }
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const title = videoTitle.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: 'unknown',
            links: [],
            category: 'liveVideo' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const title = arrangement.notes ? arrangement.notes.trim() : arrangement.title.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: 'note',
            links: [],
            category: 'liveArrangement' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const title = arrangementTitle.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: `media${mediaIdCounter++}`,
            title: title,
            type: 'note',
            links: [],
            category: 'liveArrangement' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }
});

// 3. media-master.jsonï¼ˆæ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã€é‡è¤‡ãªã—ã€åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ä¿æŒï¼‰
const mediaMaster = Array.from(mediaItems.values());

// 4. tours-media.jsonï¼ˆå‚ç…§é–¢ä¿‚ã€æ–°ã—ã„IDã§æ›´æ–°ã€åˆ†é¡åˆ¥ï¼‰
const toursMedia = toursContent.map(tour => {
  const result = {
    id: tour.id,
    liveVideoIds: [], // liveVideoç”¨ã®IDãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆ
    liveArrangementIds: [] // liveArrangementç”¨ã®IDãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆ
  };

  // liveVideosã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const title = video.title.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveVideoIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveVideoIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const title = videoTitle.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveVideoIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveVideoIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const title = arrangement.notes ? arrangement.notes.trim() : arrangement.title.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveArrangementIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveArrangementIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const title = arrangementTitle.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveArrangementIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveArrangementIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  return result;
});

// ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«å‡ºåŠ›
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/media-master.json', JSON.stringify(mediaMaster, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-media.json', JSON.stringify(toursMedia, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-extra-notes.json', JSON.stringify(toursExtraNotes, null, 2));

console.log('ä¿®æ­£ç‰ˆã®åˆ†å‰²ãŒå®Œäº†ã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼š');
console.log('- public/data/media-master.json');
console.log('- public/data/tours-media.json');  
console.log('- public/data/tours-extra-notes.json');
console.log(`æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã«${mediaMaster.length}ä»¶ã®ãƒ¦ãƒ‹ãƒ¼ã‚¯ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚`);
```

## **ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒƒãƒ—1: åˆ†å‰²ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‚’å†ç”Ÿæˆ**

ä½•ã‹å•é¡ŒãŒã‚ã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã§ã™ã€‚ã¾ãšå‹å®šç¾©ã‚’æ›´æ–°ã™ã‚‹å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ï¼š

  extraNotes: string;

  subtitle: string;

```typescript
    // ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’çµåˆã—ã¦Touré…åˆ—ã‚’ä½œæˆ
    console.log('ğŸ”— Merging data...');
    const tours: Tour[] = toursCore.map(core => {
      const setlist = setlistMap.get(core.id);
      const tourMedia = toursMedia.find(tm => tm.id === core.id);
      const extraNotes = extraNotesMap.get(core.id) || '';

      // åˆ†é¡åˆ¥ã«ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢æƒ…å ±ã‚’å–å¾—

## **ğŸ”§ å®Ÿè£…æ–¹æ³•**

`split-content-fixed.js`ã‚’ä¿®æ­£ã—ã¦ã€IDã‚’è‡ªå‹•ç”Ÿæˆã™ã‚‹éš›ã«ã‚ˆã‚Šåˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„åå‰ã‚’ä½¿ç”¨ã™ã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã«ã§ãã¾ã™ã€‚

### **ææ¡ˆã™ã‚‹å‘½åè¦å‰‡**

- **DVD/BD**: `summarize_1`, `summarize_2`, `seventh_heaven`, `cloud_nine`
- **TVæ”¾é€**: `vertical_infinity_tv`, `inazuma_2011_tv`
- **CD**: `under_cover_cd`, `cloud_nine_cd`
- **ç‰¹æ®Š**: `none`, `wowow_broadcast`, `fc_limited_vhs`

åˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„IDã«å¤‰æ›´ã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã‹ï¼Ÿã©ã®ã‚ˆã†ãªå‘½åè¦å‰‡ã‚’ãŠå¥½ã¿ã§ã™ã‹ï¼Ÿ

ä¾‹ãˆã°ï¼š
1. **å•†å“åãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹**: `summarize_1`, `seventh_heaven`, `under_cover_cd`
2. **ç•¥ç§°ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹**: `sum1`, `7th_heaven`, `uc_cd`
3. **å¹´ä»£ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹**: `dvd_1999`, `cd_2006`, `tv_2005`

ã©ã¡ã‚‰ãŒãŠå¥½ã¿ã§ã—ã‚‡ã†ã‹ï¼Ÿ

```typescript

  id: string;  // â† æ–‡å­—åˆ—å‹ãªã®ã§ä½•ã§ã‚‚OK

```json

"title": "T.M.Revolution DVD Series The Summary -summarize 1-"

// å¤‰æ›´æ¡ˆ
"id": "summarize_1",
"title": "T.M.Revolution DVD Series The Summary -summarize 1-"
```

---

**User**

å•†å“åãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ãŒã‚ˆã„ã§ã™ã€‚

---

**Cursor**

æ‰¿çŸ¥ã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼å•†å“åãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã§IDã‚’ç”Ÿæˆã™ã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã«ä¿®æ­£ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚

ã¾ãšã€ç¾åœ¨ã®ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã€å•†å“åã‹ã‚‰åˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„IDã‚’ç”Ÿæˆã™ã‚‹æ©Ÿèƒ½ã‚’è¿½åŠ ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚

```javascript
import fs from 'fs';

// å•†å“åã‹ã‚‰åˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„IDã‚’ç”Ÿæˆã™ã‚‹é–¢æ•°
function generateReadableId(title) {
  // ç‰¹æ®Šã‚±ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã®å‡¦ç†
  if (title === 'ç„¡ã—' || title === 'ç„¡ã—ï¼ˆDVDåŒ–ã¯ARENA Tourã®ã¿ï¼‰' || title === 'ç„¡ã—ï¼ˆDVD/BDåŒ–ã¯ARENA STYLE Versionã®ã¿ï¼‰') {
    return 'none';
  }
  if (title === '0001') {
    return 'unknown_0001';
  }
  if (title.includes('WOWOWã§ç”Ÿä¸­ç¶™')) {
    return 'wowow_broadcast';
  }

  let id = title
    // DVD Series The Summary
    .replace(/T\.M\.Revolution DVD Series The Summary -summarize (\d+)-/, 'summarize_$1')
    // SEVENTH HEAVEN
    .replace(/T\.M\.Revolution SEVENTH HEAVEN.*/, 'seventh_heaven')
    // UNDER:COVERé–¢é€£
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION '06 -UNDER:COVER-/, 'under_cover_live')
    .replace(/UNDER:COVERï¼ˆCDï¼‰/, 'under_cover_cd')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION'13 -UNDER II COVER-/, 'under_2_cover')
    // CLOUD NINEé–¢é€£
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION'11-12 -CLOUD NINE-ï¼ˆCDï¼‰/, 'cloud_nine_cd')
    // ãã®ä»–ã®å…·ä½“çš„ãªå•†å“
    .replace(/LIVE REVOLUTION COMPLETE EDITION-(\d+).*/, 'complete_edition_$1')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION '02 Bâ˜…Eâ˜…Sâ˜…T SUMMER CRUSH 2002/, 'best_summer_crush_2002')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION '05 -vertical infinity-ï¼ˆãƒ†ãƒ¬ãƒ“æ”¾é€ã®ã¿ï¼‰/, 'vertical_infinity_tv')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION '12 -15th Anniversary FINAL-/, 'anniversary_15th_final')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION'16-'17 -Route 20- LIVE AT NIPPON BUDOKAN/, 'route_20_budokan')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION '17 -20th Anniversary FINAL at Saitama Super Arena-/, 'anniversary_20th_final')
    .replace(/SONIC WARP the Visual Fields/, 'sonic_warp')
    .replace(/DOUBLE-DEALï¼ˆCDï¼‰å®Œå…¨ç”Ÿç”£é™å®šç›¤A/, 'double_deal_cd')
    .replace(/ã‚¤ãƒŠã‚ºãƒãƒ­ãƒƒã‚¯ãƒ•ã‚§ã‚¹ (\d+)/, 'inazuma_$1')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R\. LIVE REVOLUTION '(\d+) -Strikes Back ([IVX]+)-/, 'strikes_back_$2_$1')
    // ä¸€èˆ¬çš„ãªã‚¯ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ³ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—
    .replace(/T\.M\.R?\. LIVE REVOLUTION'?(\d+)-?'?(\d+)? ?-([^-]+)-?/g, '$3_$1')
    .replace(/T\.M\.R?\. LIVE REVOLUTION '(\d+) -([^-]+)-?/g, '$2_$1')
    .replace(/the end of genesis T\.M\.R\. evolution turbo type D/, 'genesis_turbo_type_d')
    // è¨˜å·ãƒ»ç‰¹æ®Šæ–‡å­—ã®é™¤å»ã¨æ­£è¦åŒ–
    .replace(/[^\w\s-]/g, '')
    .replace(/\s+/g, '_')
    .replace(/-+/g, '_')
    .replace(/_+/g, '_')
    .replace(/^_|_$/g, '')
    .toLowerCase();

  // ç©ºæ–‡å­—åˆ—ã®å ´åˆã¯fallback
  if (!id || id === '_') {
    id = title.replace(/[^\w]/g, '_').replace(/_+/g, '_').replace(/^_|_$/g, '').toLowerCase() || 'unknown_item';
  }

  return id;
}

// ç¾åœ¨ã®tours-content.jsonã‚’èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
const toursContent = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-content.json', 'utf8'));

// æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’åé›†ã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã‚’ä½œæˆï¼ˆé‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ï¼‰
const mediaItems = new Map(); // titleãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã§é‡è¤‡æ’é™¤
const usedIds = new Set(); // IDé‡è¤‡ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯ç”¨

// 1. tours-extra-notes.jsonï¼ˆextraNotesã®ã¿ï¼‰
const toursExtraNotes = toursContent.map(tour => ({
  id: tour.id,
  extraNotes: tour.extraNotes || ""
}));

// 2. æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’è§£æã—ã¦ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’æ§‹ç¯‰ï¼ˆé‡è¤‡æ’é™¤ã€åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ä¿æŒï¼‰
toursContent.forEach(tour => {
  // liveVideosã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const title = video.title.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          let id = generateReadableId(title);
          // IDé‡è¤‡ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
          let counter = 1;
          const originalId = id;
          while (usedIds.has(id)) {
            id = `${originalId}_${counter}`;
            counter++;
          }
          usedIds.add(id);

          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: id,
            title: title,
            type: video.type || 'unknown',
            links: video.links || [],
            category: 'liveVideo' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        } else {
          // æ—¢å­˜ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã®linksã‚’æ›´æ–°ï¼ˆã‚ˆã‚Šè©³ç´°ãªæƒ…å ±ãŒã‚ã‚Œã°ï¼‰
          const existing = mediaItems.get(title);
          if (video.links && video.links.length > 0 && existing.links.length === 0) {
            existing.links = video.links;
            existing.type = video.type || existing.type;
          }
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const title = videoTitle.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          let id = generateReadableId(title);
          // IDé‡è¤‡ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
          let counter = 1;
          const originalId = id;
          while (usedIds.has(id)) {
            id = `${originalId}_${counter}`;
            counter++;
          }
          usedIds.add(id);

          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: id,
            title: title,
            type: 'unknown',
            links: [],
            category: 'liveVideo' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®å‡¦ç†
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      // é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆæ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const title = arrangement.notes ? arrangement.notes.trim() : arrangement.title.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          let id = generateReadableId(title);
          // IDé‡è¤‡ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
          let counter = 1;
          const originalId = id;
          while (usedIds.has(id)) {
            id = `${originalId}_${counter}`;
            counter++;
          }
          usedIds.add(id);

          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: id,
            title: title,
            type: 'note',
            links: [],
            category: 'liveArrangement' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      // æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ï¼ˆè¤‡æ•°é …ç›®ã¯æ”¹è¡ŒåŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šï¼‰
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const title = arrangementTitle.trim();
        if (!mediaItems.has(title)) {
          let id = generateReadableId(title);
          // IDé‡è¤‡ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
          let counter = 1;
          const originalId = id;
          while (usedIds.has(id)) {
            id = `${originalId}_${counter}`;
            counter++;
          }
          usedIds.add(id);

          mediaItems.set(title, {
            id: id,
            title: title,
            type: 'note',
            links: [],
            category: 'liveArrangement' // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä¿æŒ
          });
        }
      });
    }
  }
});

// 3. media-master.jsonï¼ˆæ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã€é‡è¤‡ãªã—ã€åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ä¿æŒï¼‰
const mediaMaster = Array.from(mediaItems.values());

// 4. tours-media.jsonï¼ˆå‚ç…§é–¢ä¿‚ã€æ–°ã—ã„IDã§æ›´æ–°ã€åˆ†é¡åˆ¥ï¼‰
const toursMedia = toursContent.map(tour => {
  const result = {
    id: tour.id,
    liveVideoIds: [], // liveVideoç”¨ã®IDãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆ
    liveArrangementIds: [] // liveArrangementç”¨ã®IDãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆ
  };

  // liveVideosã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveVideos) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveVideos)) {
      tour.liveVideos.forEach(video => {
        const title = video.title.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveVideoIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveVideoIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveVideos === 'string' && tour.liveVideos.trim() !== '') {
      const videoLines = tour.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      videoLines.forEach(videoTitle => {
        const title = videoTitle.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveVideoIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveVideoIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  // liveArrangementsã®IDå‚ç…§ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  if (tour.liveArrangements) {
    if (Array.isArray(tour.liveArrangements)) {
      tour.liveArrangements.forEach(arrangement => {
        const title = arrangement.notes ? arrangement.notes.trim() : arrangement.title.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveArrangementIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveArrangementIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    } else if (typeof tour.liveArrangements === 'string' && tour.liveArrangements.trim() !== '') {
      const arrangementLines = tour.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim() !== '');
      arrangementLines.forEach(arrangementTitle => {
        const title = arrangementTitle.trim();
        const mediaItem = mediaItems.get(title);
        if (mediaItem && !result.liveArrangementIds.includes(mediaItem.id)) {
          result.liveArrangementIds.push(mediaItem.id);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  return result;
});

// ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«å‡ºåŠ›
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/media-master.json', JSON.stringify(mediaMaster, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-media.json', JSON.stringify(toursMedia, null, 2));
fs.writeFileSync('public/data/tours-extra-notes.json', JSON.stringify(toursExtraNotes, null, 2));

console.log('å•†å“åãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹IDã®åˆ†å‰²ãŒå®Œäº†ã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼š');
console.log('- public/data/media-master.json');
console.log('- public/data/tours-media.json');  
console.log('- public/data/tours-extra-notes.json');
console.log(`æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æºãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã«${mediaMaster.length}ä»¶ã®ãƒ¦ãƒ‹ãƒ¼ã‚¯ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚`);

// ç”Ÿæˆã•ã‚ŒãŸIDã®ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚’è¡¨ç¤º
console.log('\nç”Ÿæˆã•ã‚ŒãŸIDã®ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«:');
mediaMaster.slice(0, 10).forEach(item => {
  console.log(`  ${item.id} â†’ ${item.title}`);
});
```

ã§ã¯ã€å•†å“åãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã®IDã§åˆ†å‰²ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‚’å†ç”Ÿæˆã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

ç´ æ™´ã‚‰ã—ã„ã§ã™ï¼å•†å“åã‹ã‚‰åˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„IDãŒç”Ÿæˆã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸã€‚å®Ÿéš›ã«ç”Ÿæˆã•ã‚ŒãŸIDã®ã‚µãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ«ã‚’è¦‹ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

å®Œç’§ã§ã™ï¼å•†å“åã‹ã‚‰åˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„IDãŒç”Ÿæˆã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸï¼š

- `seventh_heaven` â†’ T.M.Revolution SEVENTH HEAVEN
- `under_cover_cd` â†’ UNDER:COVERï¼ˆCDï¼‰
- `cloud_nine_cd` â†’ T.M.R. LIVE REVOLUTION'11-12 -CLOUD NINE-ï¼ˆCDï¼‰
- `complete_edition_2` â†’ LIVE REVOLUTION COMPLETE EDITION-2
- `none` â†’ ç„¡ã—ï¼ˆã€Œç„¡ã—ã€ã®é …ç›®ç”¨ï¼‰

IDãŒé‡è¤‡ã™ã‚‹å ´åˆã¯è‡ªå‹•çš„ã«ç•ªå·ãŒä»˜ä¸ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ï¼ˆ`none_1`, `none_2`ãªã©ï¼‰ã€‚

é–‹ç™ºã‚µãƒ¼ãƒãƒ¼ã§ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

ãƒ“ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã‚‚æˆåŠŸã—ã¾ã—ãŸï¼å•†å“åãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã®IDã‚’ä½¿ã£ãŸåˆ†å‰²ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®å®Ÿè£…ãŒå®Œäº†ã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚

**æ”¹å–„ã•ã‚ŒãŸãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒˆï¼š**

1. **åˆ†ã‹ã‚Šã‚„ã™ã„ID**: 
   - `media1`, `media2` â†’ `summarize_1`, `seventh_heaven`, `under_cover_cd`

2. **å•†å“åã«åŸºã¥ã„ãŸå‘½åè¦å‰‡**:
   - DVD Series â†’ `summarize_1`, `summarize_2`...

   - Complete Edition â†’ `complete_edition_2`, `complete_edition_3`

3. **é‡è¤‡å‡¦ç†**: åŒã˜ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ãŒã‚ã‚‹å ´åˆã¯è‡ªå‹•çš„ã«ç•ªå·ä»˜ä¸ï¼ˆ`none`, `none_1`, `none_2`ï¼‰

4. **ç‰¹æ®Šã‚±ãƒ¼ã‚¹å‡¦ç†**: 
   - ã€Œç„¡ã—ã€â†’ `none`
   - ã€ŒWOWOWã§ç”Ÿä¸­ç¶™ã€â†’ `wowow_broadcast`
   - ä¸æ˜ãªã‚‚ã® â†’ `unknown_0001`

- **ãƒ¡ãƒªãƒƒãƒˆ**: ã‚¿ã‚°ç®¡ç†ãŒç°¡å˜ã€GA4ã¨çµ„ã¿åˆã‚ã›å¯èƒ½
- **ç”¨é€”**: è¤‡æ•°ã®ã‚¿ã‚°ã‚’ä¸€å…ƒç®¡ç†

## å®Ÿè£…æ–¹é‡ã®ææ¡ˆ

ç¾åœ¨ã®ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚’è¦‹ã‚‹ã¨ã€ã™ã§ã«Google Analyticsã®ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãŒ`index.html`ã«ä»®ã§è¨­ç½®ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ï¼ˆ`G-XXXXXXXXXX`ï¼‰ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹ã®æ‰‹é †ã§é€²ã‚ã‚‹ã“ã¨ã‚’ãŠå‹§ã‚ã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

### ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒƒãƒ—3: ã‚«ã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ ã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆè¨ˆæ¸¬

ã©ã®ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚»ã‚¹è§£æãƒ„ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã‚’ä½¿ç”¨ã—ãŸã„ã‹ã€ã¾ãŸå„ªå…ˆåº¦ã‚’æ•™ãˆã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚æœ€åˆã¯Google Analytics 4ã‹ã‚‰å§‹ã‚ã‚‹ã“ã¨ã‚’ãŠå‹§ã‚ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚

## ğŸ” ä¸»è¦ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚»ã‚¹è§£æãƒ„ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã®å°å…¥å…ˆURL

      // This script checks to see if a redirect is present in the query string,
      // converts it back into the correct url and adds it to the
      // browser's history using window.history.replaceState(...),
      // which won't cause the browser to attempt to load the new url.
      // When the single page app is loaded further down in this file,
      // the correct url will be waiting in the browser's history for
      // the single page app to route accordingly.
      (function(l) {
        if (l.search[1] === '/' ) {
          var decoded = l.search.slice(1).split('&').map(function(s) { 
            return s.replace(/~and~/g, '&')
          }).join('?');
          window.history.replaceState(null, null,
              l.pathname.slice(0, -1) + decoded + l.hash
          );
        }
      }(window.location))
    </script>

```typescriptreact
import { type Tour } from '../types/tour';

type TourCardListProps = {
  tours: Tour[];
  onCardClick: (t: Tour) => void;
};

export function TourCardList({ tours, onCardClick }: TourCardListProps) {
  return (
    <ul className="grid gap-3 mx-auto w-full">
      {tours.map(t => (
        <li
          key={t.id}
          className="border rounded p-3 flex flex-col gap-2 hover:bg-gray-100 cursor-pointer"
          onClick={() => onCardClick(t)}
        >
          {/* ID ã¨ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¾ã‚ã‚Šã¯æ¨ªä¸¦ã³ */}
          <div className="flex gap-6 items-start">
            <span className="text-6xl sm:text-7xl font-bold leading-none">
              {t.id}
            </span>
            <div className="leading-tight mt-2">
              <div className="text-lg sm:text-xl font-semibold">{t.title}</div>
              {t.subtitle && (
                <div className="tracking-wider text-base sm:text-lg">{t.subtitle}</div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
          {/* èª¬æ˜æ–‡ã¯ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ç¾¤ã®ä¸‹ã«è¡¨ç¤º */}
          <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-700 line-clamp-2">
            {t.description}
          </p>
        </li>
      ))}
    </ul>
  );
}
```

```typescriptreact

  tours: Tour[];

                                  </div>
                                );
                              } else {
                                // æ¥½æ›²ã®å ´åˆã¯ç•ªå·ä»˜ãã§è¡¨ç¤º
                                const currentNumber = trackNumber++;
                                return (
                                  <div key={index} className="text-sm leading-relaxed ml-4 flex">
                                    <span className="inline-block w-6 text-right mr-3 text-green-600 font-medium">{currentNumber}.</span>
                                    <span className="text-gray-700">{item}</span>
                                  </div>
                                );
                              }
                            })}
                          </div>
                        );
                      })()}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </section>
            )}

            {/* é–¢é€£ä½œå“æƒ…å ± */}
            {((active.releases?.length ?? 0) > 0 || active.liveVideos || active.liveArrangements) && (
              <section>
                <h3 className="font-bold text-base text-black mb-3 border-l-4 border-[#6ea7b2] pl-3">
                  é–¢é€£ä½œå“ãƒ»æ˜ åƒæƒ…å ±
                </h3>
                
                <div className="space-y-4">
                  {/* ã“ã®ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ãŒåéŒ²ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æº */}
                  {active.liveVideos && (
                    <div>
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-3 text-blue-800">ã“ã®ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ãŒåéŒ²ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æº</div>
                      <div className="space-y-2">
                        {/* æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ã®å ´åˆ */}
                        {typeof active.liveVideos === 'string' ? (
                          active.liveVideos.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim()).map((line, i) => (
                            <div key={i} className="bg-blue-50 p-3 rounded border border-blue-200">
                              <div className="text-sm text-gray-700">{line.trim()}</div>
                            </div>
                          ))
                        ) : (
                          /* é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ã®å ´åˆï¼ˆå¾“æ¥é€šã‚Šï¼‰ */
                          active.liveVideos.map((v, i) => (
                          <div key={i} className="bg-blue-50 p-3 rounded border border-blue-200">
                            <div className="mb-2">
                              <div className="font-semibold text-sm text-blue-800">{v.title}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-blue-600">({v.type})</div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                              {/* linksé…åˆ—ãŒã‚ã‚Œã°å„ªå…ˆã—ã¦è¡¨ç¤º */}
                              {Array.isArray((v as any).links) && (v as any).links.length > 0 ? (
                                (v as any).links.map((link: string, j: number) => (
                                  <a key={j} href={link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                     className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                    è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{(v as any).links.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
                                  </a>
                                ))
                              ) : v.link ? (
                                <a href={v.link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                   className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                  è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥
                                </a>
                              ) : null}
                            </div>
                          </div>
                          ))
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}
                  
                  {/* åŒã˜ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ã®æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æº */}
                  {active.liveArrangements && (
                    <div>
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-3 text-orange-800">åŒã˜ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ã®æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æº</div>
                      <div className="space-y-2">
                        {/* æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ã®å ´åˆ */}
                        {typeof active.liveArrangements === 'string' ? (
                          active.liveArrangements === 'ç„¡ã—' ? (
                            <div className="text-sm text-gray-600 bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded border">ç„¡ã—</div>
                          ) : (
                            active.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim()).map((line, i) => (
                              <div key={i} className="bg-orange-50 p-3 rounded border border-orange-200">
                                <div className="text-sm text-gray-700">{line.trim()}</div>
                              </div>
                            ))
                          )
                        ) : (
                          /* é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ã®å ´åˆï¼ˆå¾“æ¥é€šã‚Šï¼‰ */
                          active.liveArrangements.map((a, i) => (
                          a.notes === 'ç„¡ã—' ? (
                            <div key={i} className="text-sm text-gray-600 bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded border">ç„¡ã—</div>
                          ) : (
                            <div key={i} className="bg-orange-50 p-3 rounded border border-orange-200">
                              <div className="font-semibold text-sm text-orange-800">{a.title}</div>
                              {a.notes && <div className="text-xs text-orange-600 mt-1">{a.notes}</div>}
                            </div>
                          )
                          ))
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </section>
            )}
          </div>
        }
```

```typescriptreact
import { type Tour } from '../types/tour';

type TourCardListProps = {
  tours: Tour[];
  onCardClick: (t: Tour) => void;
};

export function TourCardList({ tours, onCardClick }: TourCardListProps) {
  return (
    <ul className="grid gap-3 mx-auto w-full">
      {tours.map(t => (
        <li
          key={t.id}
          className="border rounded p-3 flex flex-col gap-2 hover:bg-gray-100 cursor-pointer"
          onClick={() => onCardClick(t)}
        >
          {/* ID ã¨ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¾ã‚ã‚Šã¯æ¨ªä¸¦ã³ */}
          <div className="flex gap-6 items-start">
            <span className="text-6xl sm:text-7xl font-bold leading-none">
              {t.id}
            </span>
            <div className="leading-tight mt-2">
              <div className="text-lg sm:text-xl font-semibold">{t.title}</div>
              {t.subtitle && (
                <div className="tracking-wider text-base sm:text-lg">{t.subtitle}</div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
          {/* èª¬æ˜æ–‡ã¯ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ç¾¤ã®ä¸‹ã«è¡¨ç¤º */}
          <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-700 line-clamp-2">
            {t.description}
          </p>
        </li>
      ))}
    </ul>
  );
}

### **ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®æµã‚Œ**

1. **tours-media.json** ã‹ã‚‰å„å…¬æ¼”ã®ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢IDãƒªã‚¹ãƒˆã‚’å–å¾—

   - **å•†å“å**: `v.title` ï¼ˆmedia-master.jsonã®`title`ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ï¼‰
   - **å•†å“åã®èª¬æ˜**: `v.type` ï¼ˆmedia-master.jsonã®`type`ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ï¼‰

### **è¡¨ç¤ºä¾‹ã®åˆ†æ**

ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ³ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒƒãƒˆã®ID21ã®å ´åˆï¼š
- **tours-media.json**: `"liveVideoIds": ["none"]`
- **media-master.json**: 
  ```json

## **Option C: æ··åˆã‚¢ãƒ—ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ**

### **å®Ÿè£…ä¸Šã®å¤‰æ›´ç‚¹ï¼ˆOption Aæ¡ç”¨ã®å ´åˆï¼‰**

2. **tours-media.json**: `liveVideoNote`, `liveArrangementNote` ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰è¿½åŠ

### **ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ç§»è¡Œä¾‹**

**Before**:

### **Step 4: dataService.ts ã®æ›´æ–°**

dataServiceã‚’æ›´æ–°ã—ã¦æ–°ã—ã„è£œè¶³æƒ…å ±ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã«å¯¾å¿œã•ã›ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

dataService.tsã‚’æ›´æ–°ã—ã¦ã€æ–°ã—ã„è£œè¶³æƒ…å ±ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã‚’ã‚µãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

```typescript
import type { Tour } from '../types/tour';
import type { MediaItem, TourMedia, TourExtraNotes, TourCore, Setlist } from '../types/media';

export async function loadToursData(): Promise<Tour[]> {
  const version = import.meta.env?.VITE_APP_VERSION || Date.now();
  
  console.log('ğŸ”„ Loading tours data from split files...');
  
  try {
    // ä¸¦è¡Œã—ã¦ã™ã¹ã¦ã®JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‚’å–å¾—
    console.log('ğŸ“¥ Fetching data files...');
    const [
      toursCore,
      setlists,
      mediaMaster,
      toursMedia,
      toursExtraNotes
    ] = await Promise.all([
      fetch(`data/tours-core.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourCore[]>,
      fetch(`data/setlists.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<Setlist[]>,
      fetch(`data/media-master.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<MediaItem[]>,
      fetch(`data/tours-media.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourMedia[]>,
      fetch(`data/tours-extra-notes.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as Promise<TourExtraNotes[]>
    ]);

    console.log(`âœ… Data loaded: ${toursCore.length} tours, ${setlists.length} setlists, ${mediaMaster.length} media items`);

    // ã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ‡ãƒƒã‚¯ã‚¹ãƒãƒƒãƒ—ã‚’ä½œæˆï¼ˆé«˜é€ŸåŒ–ã®ãŸã‚ï¼‰
    const setlistMap = new Map(setlists.map(s => [s.tourId, s.songs]));
    const mediaMap = new Map(mediaMaster.map(m => [m.id, m]));
    const extraNotesMap = new Map(toursExtraNotes.map(en => [en.id, en.extraNotes]));

    // ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’çµåˆã—ã¦Touré…åˆ—ã‚’ä½œæˆ
    console.log('ğŸ”— Merging data...');
    const tours: Tour[] = toursCore.map(core => {
      const setlist = setlistMap.get(core.id);
      const tourMedia = toursMedia.find(tm => tm.id === core.id);
      const extraNotes = extraNotesMap.get(core.id) || '';

      // åˆ†é¡åˆ¥ã«ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢æƒ…å ±ã‚’å–å¾—
      const liveVideoIds = tourMedia?.liveVideoIds || [];
      const liveArrangementIds = tourMedia?.liveArrangementIds || [];
      
      const liveVideos = liveVideoIds.map(id => mediaMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean) as MediaItem[];
      const liveArrangements = liveArrangementIds.map(id => mediaMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean) as MediaItem[];

      return {
        id: core.id,
        title: core.title,
        subtitle: core.subtitle,
        year: core.year,
        description: core.description,
        setlist: setlist || [],
        extraNotes,
        // åˆ†é¡æƒ…å ±ã‚’ä½¿ã£ã¦æ­£ã—ãåˆ†ã‘ã¦é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ã§è¿”ã™
        liveVideos: liveVideos.length > 0 ? liveVideos.map(v => ({
          title: v.title,
          type: v.type as 'DVD' | 'Blu-ray' | 'YouTube' | 'é…ä¿¡' | 'TV' | 'VHS',
          links: v.links || []
        })) : undefined,
        liveArrangements: liveArrangements.length > 0 ? liveArrangements.map(a => ({
          title: a.title,
          type: a.type as 'CD' | 'DVD' | 'TV' | 'é…ä¿¡',
          notes: a.title
        })) : undefined,
        // æ–°ã—ã„è£œè¶³æƒ…å ±ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰
        liveVideoNote: tourMedia?.liveVideoNote,
        liveArrangementNote: tourMedia?.liveArrangementNote,
        // å¿…è¦ã«å¿œã˜ã¦ä»–ã®ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã‚‚è¿½åŠ 
        memo: '',
        releases: []
      };
    });

    console.log(`âœ… Successfully merged ${tours.length} tours`);
    return tours;

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ Failed to load tours data:', error);
    // ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒãƒƒã‚¯: å¾“æ¥ã®tours.jsonã‚’è©¦ã™
    try {
      console.log('ğŸ”„ Trying fallback tours.json...');
      const fallbackData = await fetch(`tours.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json());
      console.warn('âš ï¸ Using fallback tours.json');
      return fallbackData;
    } catch (fallbackError) {
      console.error('âŒ Fallback also failed:', fallbackError);
      return [];
    }
  }
}

// ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢æƒ…å ±ã‚’å–å¾—ã™ã‚‹ãƒ˜ãƒ«ãƒ‘ãƒ¼é–¢æ•°
export async function getMediaItems(mediaIds: string[]): Promise<MediaItem[]> {
  const version = import.meta.env?.VITE_APP_VERSION || Date.now();
  
  try {
    const mediaMaster = await fetch(`data/media-master.json?v=${version}`).then(r => r.json()) as MediaItem[];
    const mediaMap = new Map(mediaMaster.map(m => [m.id, m]));
    
    return mediaIds.map(id => mediaMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean) as MediaItem[];
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to load media data:', error);
    return [];
  }
}
```

### **Step 5: Tourå‹å®šç¾©ã®æ›´æ–°**

Tourå‹ã«æ–°ã—ã„ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã‚’è¿½åŠ ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

  id: number;

  subtitle: string;
  year: number;
  description: string;
  setlist?: string[];
  extraNotes?: string;
  memo?: string;
  releases?: {

    type: 'album' | 'single';
    releaseDate: string;
    link?: string;
    coverImageUrl?: string;

    title: string;
    link?: string;

    notes?: string;
    links?: string[];
  }[];

                            <div className="mb-2">
                              <div className="font-semibold text-sm">{v.title}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">({v.type})</div>
                            </div>
                            {/* ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯ãƒœã‚¿ãƒ³ã¯ä¸€æ™‚çš„ã«éè¡¨ç¤º */}
                            {/* <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                              {Array.isArray((v as any).links) && (v as any).links.length > 0 ? (
                                (v as any).links.map((link: string, j: number) => (
                                  <a key={j} href={link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                     className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                    è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥{(v as any).links.length > 1 ? `(${j + 1})` : ''}
                                  </a>
                                ))
                              ) : v.link ? (
                                <a href={v.link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" 
                                   className="px-3 py-1 bg-blue-600 text-white text-xs rounded hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">
                                  è¦–è´/è³¼å…¥
                                </a>
                              ) : null}
                            </div> */}
                          </div>
                          ))
                        )}
                      </div>
                    ) : active.liveVideoNote ? (
                      <div className="bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded border">
                        <div className="font-semibold text-sm">ç„¡ã—</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">ï¼ˆ{active.liveVideoNote}ï¼‰</div>
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-600">ç„¡ã—</div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )}
                
                {/* åŒã˜ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ã®æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æº */}
                {(active.liveArrangements || active.liveArrangementNote) && (
                  <div className="mb-4">
                    <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-2">ãƒ»åŒã˜ãƒ©ã‚¤ãƒ–ã‚¢ãƒ¬ãƒ³ã‚¸ã®æ˜ åƒãƒ»éŸ³æº</div>
                    {active.liveArrangements ? (
                      <div className="space-y-2">
                        {/* æ–‡å­—åˆ—å½¢å¼ã®å ´åˆ */}
                        {typeof active.liveArrangements === 'string' ? (
                          active.liveArrangements === 'ç„¡ã—' ? (
                            <div className="text-sm text-gray-600">ç„¡ã—</div>
                          ) : (
                            active.liveArrangements.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim()).map((line, i) => (
                              <div key={i} className="bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded border">
                                <div className="text-sm">{line.trim()}</div>
                              </div>
                            ))
                          )
                        ) : (
                          /* é…åˆ—å½¢å¼ã®å ´åˆï¼ˆtypeã‚’è¿½åŠ ï¼‰ */
                          active.liveArrangements.map((a, i) => (
                          <div key={i} className="bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded border">
                            <div className="mb-2">
                              <div className="font-semibold text-sm">{a.title}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">({a.type})</div>
                            </div>
                            {a.notes && <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">{a.notes}</div>}
                          </div>
                          ))
                        )}
                      </div>
                    ) : active.liveArrangementNote ? (
                      <div className="bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded border">
                        <div className="font-semibold text-sm">ç„¡ã—</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">ï¼ˆ{active.liveArrangementNote}ï¼‰</div>
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-600">ç„¡ã—</div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )}
```

## ç¾åœ¨ã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿æ§‹é€ ã®å•é¡Œç‚¹

1. **ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®é‡è¤‡ãƒ»ä¸æ•´åˆ**
   - Tour ID 1ã§`summarize_1`ãŒ`liveVideoIds`ã¨`liveArrangementIds`ã®ä¸¡æ–¹ã«å­˜åœ¨

2. **ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã®åˆ†é¡å•é¡Œ**
   - `media-master.json`ã§`category`ã‚’`liveVideo`/`liveArrangement`ã§åˆ†ã‘ã¦ã„ã‚‹ã®ã«ã€`tours-media.json`ã§ã¯æ‰‹å‹•ã§åˆ†é¡ã—ã¦ã„ã‚‹
   - åŒã˜ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ãŒç•°ãªã‚‹ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªã§ä½¿ã‚ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹

3. **ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®è«–ç†çš„ä¸æ•´åˆ**
   - `media-master.json`ã§`summarize_1`ã¯`category: "liveVideo"`ãªã®ã«ã€Tour ID 1ã§ã¯`liveArrangementIds`ã«ã‚‚å«ã¾ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹

ã“ã‚Œã‚‰ã‚’è€ƒæ…®ã™ã‚‹ã¨ã€**å…ƒã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãŒã©ã†ã‚ã‚‹ã¹ãã‹**ã‚’æ•´ç†ã™ã‚‹å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ï¼š

```markdown
# T.M.Revolution Tour Data æ§‹é€ åˆ†æãƒ¬ãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆ

## ç¾åœ¨ã®å•é¡Œç‚¹

### 1. ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®é‡è¤‡ãƒ»ä¸æ•´åˆ
- Tour ID 1: `summarize_1`ãŒ`liveVideoIds`ã¨`liveArrangementIds`ã®ä¸¡æ–¹ã«å­˜åœ¨

  // liveVideoIds ã®ç¢ºèª
  tour.liveVideoIds.forEach(id => {
    const media = mediaMap.get(id);
    if (media && media.category !== 'liveVideo') {
      console.log(`âš ï¸  Tour ${tour.id}: ${id} ã¯${media.category}ã ãŒ liveVideoIds ã§ä½¿ç”¨`);
    }
  });
  
  // liveArrangementIds ã®ç¢ºèª

      console.log(`âš ï¸  Tour ${tour.id}: ${id} ã¯${media.category}ã ãŒ liveArrangementIds ã§ä½¿ç”¨`);
    }
  });
});

// 2. é‡è¤‡ä½¿ç”¨ã®æ¤œå‡º
console.log('\nğŸ”„ é‡è¤‡ä½¿ç”¨ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯:');

const arrangementUsage = new Map();

  tour.liveVideoIds.forEach(id => {
    if (!videoUsage.has(id)) videoUsage.set(id, []);
    videoUsage.get(id).push(tour.id);
  });
  
  tour.liveArrangementIds.forEach(id => {
    if (!arrangementUsage.has(id)) arrangementUsage.set(id, []);
    arrangementUsage.get(id).push(tour.id);
  });
});

// é‡è¤‡ä½¿ç”¨ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã‚‹ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚’è¡¨ç¤º

  if (tours.length > 1) {
    console.log(`ğŸ“¹ ${mediaId}: Tours ${tours.join(', ')} ã§é‡è¤‡ä½¿ç”¨`);
  }
});

  if (tours.length > 1) {
    console.log(`ğŸµ ${mediaId}: Tours ${tours.join(', ')} ã§é‡è¤‡ä½¿ç”¨`);
  }
});

// 3. ä¿®æ­£ææ¡ˆã®ç”Ÿæˆ

const tour1 = toursMedia.find(t => t.id === 1);
if (tour1) {
  const summarize1Media = mediaMap.get('summarize_1');
  if (summarize1Media) {
    console.log(`\nä¿®æ­£ Tour 1:`);
    console.log(`- summarize_1 ã¯ category: ${summarize1Media.category}`);
    
    if (summarize1Media.category === 'liveVideo') {
      console.log(`- liveArrangementIds ã‹ã‚‰ summarize_1 ã‚’å‰Šé™¤ã™ã¹ã`);
      tour1.liveArrangementIds = tour1.liveArrangementIds.filter(id => id !== 'summarize_1');
    } else {
      console.log(`- liveVideoIds ã‹ã‚‰ summarize_1 ã‚’å‰Šé™¤ã™ã¹ã`);  
      tour1.liveVideoIds = tour1.liveVideoIds.filter(id => id !== 'summarize_1');
    }
  }

// 5. ä½¿ç”¨ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ãªã„ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ ã®æ¤œå‡º

  tour.liveVideoIds.forEach(id => usedMediaIds.add(id));
  tour.liveArrangementIds.forEach(id => usedMediaIds.add(id));

if (unusedMedia.length > 0) {

å‡ºåŠ›ãŒå°‘ãªã„ã‚ˆã†ã§ã™ã€‚è©³ã—ãç¢ºèªã™ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã«å‡ºåŠ›ã‚’æ”¹å–„ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚ã¾ãšã€ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ãŒå­˜åœ¨ã™ã‚‹ã‹ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

ãƒãƒƒã‚¯ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ãŒè¦‹å½“ãŸã‚‰ãªã„ã®ã§ã€ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã®çµæœã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚ã¾ãšã€åª’ä½“ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®å¤§ãã•ã‚’è¦‹ã¦ã¿ã‚‹ã¨ã€`media-master.json`ã¨`tour-media.json`ã¯ä»¥å‰ã‚ˆã‚Šå°ã•ããªã£ã¦ã„ã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã§ã™ã€‚ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®æ¤œè¨¼ã‚’åˆ¥ã®ã‚¢ãƒ—ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒã§è¡Œã£ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

```javascript
import fs from 'fs';

try {
  console.log('ğŸ“Š ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«æ¤œè¨¼é–‹å§‹...\n');
  
  // ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«å­˜åœ¨ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
  const files = [
    'public/data/media-master.json',
    'public/data/tours-media.json',
    'public/data/tours-core.json',
    'public/data/setlists.json'
  ];
  
  files.forEach(file => {
    if (fs.existsSync(file)) {
      const stats = fs.statSync(file);
      console.log(`âœ… ${file}: ${stats.size} bytes`);
    } else {
      console.log(`âŒ ${file}: è¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“`);
    }
  });
  
  // ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
  const mediaMaster = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/media-master.json', 'utf8'));
  const toursMedia = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('public/data/tours-media.json', 'utf8'));
  
  console.log('\nğŸ“ˆ ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿çµ±è¨ˆ:');
  console.log(`- ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ãƒã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ¼: ${mediaMaster.length} ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ `);
  console.log(`- ãƒ„ã‚¢ãƒ¼ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢: ${toursMedia.length} ãƒ„ã‚¢ãƒ¼`);
  
  // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ†å¸ƒ
  const categories = {};
  mediaMaster.forEach(m => {
    categories[m.category] = (categories[m.category] || 0) + 1;
  });
  
  console.log('\nğŸ·ï¸  ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ†å¸ƒ:');
  Object.entries(categories).forEach(([cat, count]) => {
    console.log(`- ${cat}: ${count} ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ `);
  });
  
  // ä¸æ•´åˆãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
  console.log('\nğŸ” ä¸æ•´åˆãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯:');
  const mediaMap = new Map(mediaMaster.map(m => [m.id, m]));
  let inconsistencies = 0;
  
  toursMedia.forEach(tour => {
    // liveVideoIds ã®ç¢ºèª
    tour.liveVideoIds?.forEach(id => {
      const media = mediaMap.get(id);
      if (!media) {
        console.log(`âŒ Tour ${tour.id}: ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ID "${id}" ãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“`);
        inconsistencies++;
      } else if (media.category !== 'liveVideo') {
        console.log(`âš ï¸  Tour ${tour.id}: "${id}" ã¯${media.category}ã ãŒliveVideoIdsã§ä½¿ç”¨`);
        inconsistencies++;
      }
    });
    
    // liveArrangementIds ã®ç¢ºèª
    tour.liveArrangementIds?.forEach(id => {
      const media = mediaMap.get(id);
      if (!media) {
        console.log(`âŒ Tour ${tour.id}: ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ID "${id}" ãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“`);
        inconsistencies++;
      } else if (media.category !== 'liveArrangement') {
        console.log(`âš ï¸  Tour ${tour.id}: "${id}" ã¯${media.category}ã ãŒliveArrangementIdsã§ä½¿ç”¨`);
        inconsistencies++;
      }
    });
  });
  
  if (inconsistencies === 0) {
    console.log('âœ… ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿æ•´åˆæ€§: å•é¡Œãªã—');
  } else {
    console.log(`âŒ ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿æ•´åˆæ€§: ${inconsistencies} ä»¶ã®å•é¡Œ`);
  }
  
  console.log('\nğŸ‰ æ¤œè¨¼å®Œäº†!');
  
} catch (error) {
  console.error('âŒ ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼:', error.message);
}
```

ä½•ã‚‚å‡ºåŠ›ã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ãªã„ã®ã¯å¥‡å¦™ã§ã™ã­ã€‚ç›´æ¥ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«å†…å®¹ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

è‰¯ã„ã§ã™ã­ï¼ä¿®æ­£ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆãŒå‹•ä½œã—ã¦ã€Tour ID 1ã®`liveArrangementIds`ã‹ã‚‰`summarize_1`ãŒå‰Šé™¤ã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸã€‚ç¾åœ¨ã¯`liveVideoIds`ã®ã¿ã«å­˜åœ¨ã—ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚
